(function($){
	$.getUrlParams = function(){
		var ret = {},
		seg = window.location.search.replace(/^\?/,'').replace(/%7C/g, '|').split('&amp;'),
		len = seg.length, i = 0, s;
		for (;i&lt;len;i++) {
			if (!seg[i]) { continue; }
			s = seg[i].split('=');
			ret[s[0]] = s[1];
		}
		return ret;
	}
})(jQuery);
$("#selection .subarea .nearsq input:checkbox").click(function(){
    if(!this.checked)return;
    var sc = $('#selection .subarea .nearsq input:checkbox[checked]');
    var count =  sc.length;    
    if(count &gt; 4) {
        alert('最多选择4个商圈。');
        return false;
    }
});
var subsq = function(){
    boot.require('util.uri', function(Frame, uri){
		var sc = $('#selection .subarea .nearsq input:checkbox[checked]'),
			url = new uri(),
			local = url.path.local;
		if(local) {
			local = local.split('_').slice(0,1);
		} else {
			local = [];
		}
		
		for(var i = 0, leni = sc.length; i &lt; leni; i ++) {
			local.push(sc[i].value);
		}
		url.path.local = local.join('_');
		location.href = url.toString().replace(/\/pn\d+/, '');
	});    
};
</script>

	boot.require('util.uri', function(Frame, uri){

	    var mutex = mutexs[i];

	    for(var j = 0, lenj = mutex.params.length; j &lt; lenj; j ++) {
	        pobj[mutex.params[j]] = null;

<script type="text/javascript">
	$(function(){
		showpinpaihouse();
		//品牌房源筛选
		function showpinpaihouse(){    
	        var showpinpai = $("#ispinpai");    
	        if(showpinpai){    
	            // 选中品牌房源 
	            if(location.search.indexOf("param9310=1")&gt;-1){    
	            	showpinpai.attr("checked","true");    
	            }    
	            showpinpai.click(function() {    
	                var pinpai = "param9310=1",url = location.href;    
	                if(showpinpai.attr("checked")) {    
	                    var sUpara = "";    
	                    if(url.indexOf(pinpai) == -1){    
	                        sUpara = url.indexOf("?")== -1 ? "?" : "&amp;";    
	                        location.href = url.replace(/pn\d+\//i,"")+sUpara+pinpai;    
	                    }    
	                }else{    
	                    if (url.indexOf(pinpai) != -1) {    
	                        if (url.indexOf("?param9310=1&amp;") != -1) {    
	                            url = url.replace("param9310=1&amp;", "");    
	                        }
	                        url = url.replace("?param9310=1", "").replace("&amp;param9310=1", "").replace("param9310=1", "");
	                        location.href = url.replace(/pn\d+\//i,"");    
	                    }    
	                }    
	        
	            });    
	        }    
	    }
		
	});
</script>

        var par_old_zindex ;
        $('.more_filter_cn .fake_select_item').bind('mouseenter',function(){
            $(this).addClass('open');
            var par = $('#selection'),filter = $('#filter'),zindex = parseInt(filter.css('z-index'));
            par_old_zindex = parseInt(par.css('z-index'))||1;
            par.css('z-index',zindex+1);
            
        }).bind('mouseleave',function(){
            $(this).removeClass('open');
            $(this).find('.select_lst_cn a[status="select"]').addClass('select');
            $(this).find('.select_lst_cn a[status="icon_check_on"]').addClass('icon_check_on');
            $('#selection').css('z-index',par_old_zindex);
        });
		$('.select_lst_cn a').bind('mouseenter',function(){
           $(this).siblings('.icon_check_on').removeClass('icon_check_on').attr('status','icon_check_on');
           $(this).siblings('.select').removeClass('select').attr('status','select');
        });

	//筛选条件-checkbox
	$('#buildingera a[data-para-value],#floor a[data-para-value],#fittype a[data-para-value]').click(function(){
		var key = $(this).parents('.secitem').attr('data-para-key');
		var val = $(this).attr('data-para-value');
		var url_params = $.getUrlParams();
		var url_value = url_params[key] ? url_params[key] + '|' : '';
		//删除，重新赋值
		delete url_params[key];
		if(val){
			val += '|';
		}
		//如果已经在筛选条件中则删除 | hack of '1|'-&gt;-4_-1|
		if(val &amp;&amp; ('|' + url_value).indexOf('|' + val) &gt; -1){
			url_value = url_value.replace(val, '');
		}
		//否则添加到最后
		else{
			url_value += val;
		}
		url_value = url_value.substring(0, url_value.length - 1);
		if(url_value){
			url_params[key] = url_value;
		}
		var url = location.href.replace(/\?.*/, '');
		if(!$.isEmptyObject(url_params)){
			var arr = [];
			for(var o in url_params){
				arr.push(o + '=' + url_params[o]);
			}
			url += '?' + arr.join('&amp;');
		}
		location.href = url.replace(/%7C/g, '|').replace(/\/pn\d+/, '');
		return false;
	});

	$('#minprice_filter1 :button,#minprice_filter2 :button,#minprice_filter3 :button,#area_filter :button,#tingshi_filter :button').click(function(){
		var inputs = $(this).parents('.prifilter').find('input[para]');
		if($(this).val() == "查找")
		{
			inputs = $(this).parents('.shoufu').find('input[para]');
		}
		
		var url = window.location.href.substring(7);
		var url_pre = location.hostname;
		var url_middle = location.pathname;
		//点击价格、面积筛选的时候需要将url中的h1、k1替换成空；
		var replace_reg = {
			//huansuan:/i\d+(\/)?/,
			huansuanyue:/i\d+(\/)?/,
			area:/k\d+(\/)?/,
			huxingshi:/e\d+(\/)?/
		};
		//如果点击排序之后需要加此默认的筛选条件
		var default_cond = {
			huansuan:'0.05_20',
			huansuanyue:'2_*',
			area:'2_*'
		};
		
		var _paras = {};
		$.each(inputs, function(i, item){
			var para = $(item).attr('para');
			if(replace_reg[para] &amp;&amp; '' != $(item).val()){
				url_middle = url_middle.replace(replace_reg[para], '');
			}
			if(!_paras[para])
			{
				_paras[para] = [];
			}
			if($(item).val() == "输入首付")
			{
				$(item).attr("value","0");
			};
			_paras[para].push($(item).val());
		});
		var paras = $.getUrlParams();
		//针对huansuanyue和huansuan互斥做特殊处理
		/*if($('#filter_huansuan').val() == '1'){
			delete paras['huansuan'];
		}else if($('#filter_huansuan').val() == '2'){
			delete paras['huansuanyue'];
		}*/
		//如果价格的参数是下面的排序带的，则去掉sort_hack=1标识
		/*if('1' == paras['sort_hack']){
			var val = $(this).attr('value');
			if('价格筛选' == val &amp;&amp; paras['huansuanyue']){
				delete paras['sort_hack'];
			}
			else if('面积筛选' == val &amp;&amp; paras['area']){
				delete paras['sort_hack'];
			}
		}*/
		var huansuanyueOffset = 1, huansuanOffset = 10000;
		if($("#minprice_filter3 :text").val() != "输入首付")
		{
			if(!_paras["bunengdaikuan"])
			{
				_paras["bunengdaikuan"] = [];
			}
			_paras["bunengdaikuan"].push(0);
		};
		
		for(var o in _paras){
			var sort_hack = paras['sort_hack'];
			if(2 == _paras[o].length){
				var offset = 1;
				if(o == 'huansuanyue'){
					offset = huansuanyueOffset;
				}
				else if(o == 'huansuan'){
					offset = huansuanOffset;
				}
				
				var val0 = 0;
				if(_paras[o][0]){
					val0 = _paras[o][0] - 0;
				}
				if(sort_hack &amp;&amp; default_cond[o]){
					var values = default_cond[o].split('_');
					values[0] = values[0] - 0;
					if(values[0] &gt; val0)
					val0 = values[0];
				}
				if(offset != 1)
					_paras[o][0] = Math.round(val0 * offset);
				else
					_paras[o][0] = val0;
				
				var val1 = '*';
				if(_paras[o][1]){
					val1 = _paras[o][1];
				}
				if('*' != val1 &amp;&amp; sort_hack &amp;&amp; default_cond[o]){
					val1 = val1 - 0;
					var values = default_cond[o].split('_');
					if(values[1] &lt; val1)
					val1 = values[1];
				}
				if('*' != val1 &amp;&amp; offset != 1)
					val1 = Math.round(val1 * offset);
				_paras[o][1] = val1;
				
				paras[o] = _paras[o].join('_');
			}
			else{
				if(sort_hack &amp;&amp; default_cond[o]){
					var val = paras[o];
					if(val)
						val = val - 0;
						
					var values = default_cond[o].split('_');
					values[0] = values[0] - 0;
					if(values[0] &gt; val)
						val = values[0];
					if('*' != values[1]){
						values[1] = values[1] - 0;
						if(values[1] &lt; val)
							val = values[1];
					}
					paras[o] = val;
				}
				else{
					paras[o] = _paras[o][0];
					if('' == _paras[o][0]){
						delete paras[o];
					}
				}
			}
			paras[o] = _paras[o].join('_');
		}
		
		var url = 'http://' + url_pre + url_middle;
		if(!$.isEmptyObject(paras)){
			url += '?' + $.param(paras);
		}
		location.href = url.replace(/%7C/g, '|').replace(/\/pn\d+/, '');
	});
	
</script>

					var default_cond = {
						huansuan:{min:0.05,max:20,multi:10000},
						huansuanyue:{min:2,multi:1,mutex:/i\d+(\/)?/},
						area:{min:2,multi:1,mutex:/k\d+(\/)?/}
					};
					
					//给右边三个排序按钮赋title
                    var sort_enum = ['area', 'huansuanyue', 'huansuan'];
                    var tbfilter_sort = $('.tbfilter span a');

					for(var idx = 0, len = tbfilter_sort.length ; idx &lt; len ; idx ++){
                        var pathname = location.pathname, url = 'http://' + location.hostname + pathname;
                        var _url_paras = $.getUrlParams(), _sort = (_url_paras['sort'] || '_').split('_');
						var s = tbfilter_sort.get(idx);
						var __sort = [_sort[0], ''], currentSort = _sort[1];
						if(_sort[0] != sort_enum[idx]){
							__sort[0] = sort_enum[idx];
							//面积默认降序，其他默认升序
							__sort[1] = 'asc';
							if(__sort[0] == 'area'){
								__sort[1] = 'desc';
							}
							currentSort = __sort[1];
						}
						else{
                            $(s).attr('hasChecked',idx);
                            $(s).attr('_sort',_sort[1]);
							//相反排序
							__sort[1] = _sort[1] == 'asc' ? 'desc' : 'asc';
						}
						_url_paras['sort'] = __sort[0] + '_' + __sort[1];
						
						var k = __sort[0];
						if(default_cond[k]){
							_url_paras['sort_hack'] = 1;
							for(var o in default_cond){
								if(default_cond[o].mutex &amp;&amp; default_cond[o].mutex.test(pathname))
									continue;
								var values = _url_paras[o];
								var min = default_cond[o].min;
								var max = default_cond[o].max;
								var multi = default_cond[o].multi;
								if(!values){
									values = [];
									if(min){
										values.push(min * multi);
									}
									else{
										values.push(0);
									}
									if(max){
										values.push(max * multi);
									}
									else{
										values.push('*');
									}
								}
								else{
									values = values.split('_');
									if(min &amp;&amp; (min * multi) &gt; values[0]){
										values[0] = min * multi;
									}
									if('*' != values[1]){
										if(max &amp;&amp; values[1] &gt; max * multi){
										values[1] = max * multi;
									}
									}
								}
								_url_paras[o] = values[0] + '_' + values[1];
							}		
						}
						if(!$.isEmptyObject(_url_paras)){
							url += '?' + $.param(_url_paras);
						}
						
						//替换分页参数
						url = url.replace(/\/pn\d+/, '').replace(/%7C/g, '|');
						var order = __sort[0] + '_' + __sort[1];
						$(s).attr({'href':url,'title':'切换至'+sort_map[order]})
							.click(function(){
								for(var m in gaq_map){
									if($(this).attr('href').indexOf(m) == -1)
										continue;
									var city = ____json4fe.locallist[0].listname;
									var yiji = ____json4fe.catentry[0].listname;
									var erji = ____json4fe.catentry[1].listname;
									var info = '/' + city + '/' + yiji + '/' + erji + '/';
									_gaq.push(['pageTracker._trackEvent', 'list', gaq_map[m], info]);
								}
							});
					}
                    tbfilter_sort.each(function(){
                        var num=$(this).attr('hasChecked');
                        var sort=$(this).attr('_sort');
                        var downcls,oncls,ncls,hoverCls,defultCls;
                        if(num){
                            num=num-0+2;
                            downcls=sort=='desc'?'1_on':'_on';
                            oncls=sort!=='desc'?'1_on':'_on';
                            ncls=sort!=='desc'?'n1':'n';
                            hoverCls='sort_icon'+num+oncls;
                            defultCls='sort_icon'+num+downcls;
                            if(num==2){
                                hoverCls='sort_icon2_'+ncls+' sort_icon2'+oncls;
                                defultCls='sort_icon2_'+ncls+' sort_icon'+num+downcls;
                            }
                            $(this).addClass(defultCls);
                            $(this).attr('defultCls',defultCls);
                            $(this).attr('hoverCls',hoverCls);
                        }

                    });
                    tbfilter_sort.live({mouseenter:function(){
                        var hoverCls=$(this).attr('hoverCls'),defultCls=$(this).attr('defultCls');
                        defultCls&amp;&amp;$(this).removeClass(defultCls).addClass(hoverCls);},
                     mouseleave:function(){
                        var hoverCls=$(this).attr('hoverCls'),defultCls=$(this).attr('defultCls');
                        hoverCls&amp;&amp;$(this).removeClass(hoverCls).addClass(defultCls);
                    }})
				})();
				</script>
</div>
</div>

<script>
			$.getJSON(
				"http://house.focus.cn/common/newhouse/api/loupandataforinfolist.api.php?city_id=1&amp;callback=?",
				function(data){
					if(!data || !data.items)
						return;
					var html = [];
					$(data.items).each(function(i, item){
						var key = '', value = '';
						for(var o in item){
							key = o;
							value = item[o];
						}
						html.push('&lt;li&gt;&lt;a target="_blank" href="' + value + '"&gt;北京' + key + '&lt;/a&gt;&lt;/li&gt;');
					});
					$('#newhouse').show().find('dd').html(html.join(''));
				}
			);
		</script>

			});

	}

		span_img.show();
	}
},function(){
